# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="31a56-105">Membros obsoletos no .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="31a56-105">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="31a56-106">Este artigo lista os membros de tipo que estão obsoletos no .NET Framework 4,5 e versões posteriores.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="31a56-106">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="31a56-107">Membros de tipo são agrupados por assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="31a56-107">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="31a56-108">Este artigo não lista os membros de tipos obsoletos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="31a56-108">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="31a56-109">Para obter uma lista de tipos obsoletos, consulte [tipos obsoletos](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="31a56-109">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

## <a name="iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="31a56-1111">IEHost.dll e IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="31a56-1111">IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="31a56-1112">Os assemblies IEHost.dll e IEExec.exe foram removidos do .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="31a56-1112">The IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe assemblies have been removed from .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="31a56-1113">Todos os seus tipos e seus membros são obsoletos e não têm suporte no .NET Framework 4,5 e posterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="31a56-1113">All of their types and their members are obsolete and are not supported in .NET Framework 4.5 and later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="31a56-1114">Esses assemblies foram usados para hospedar controles de Windows Forms e executar executáveis no Internet Explorer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="31a56-1114">These assemblies were used to host Windows Forms controls and to run executables in Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="31a56-1115">Entre as alternativas a essa tecnologia estão ClickOnce, XBAP (Aplicativos de Navegador XAML) e Microsoft Silverlight.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="31a56-1115">Alternatives to this technology include ClickOnce, XAML Browser Applications (XBAP), and Microsoft Silverlight.</span></span>
